   </span>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th rowspan="4">\n         <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Super_High_Frequency" title="Super High Frequency">\n          SHF\n         </a>\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         <b>\n          <a href="/wiki/9-centimeter_band" title="9-centimeter band">\n           9 cm\n          </a>\n         </b>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <span class="nowrap">\n          3.400 GHz \xe2\x80\x93 3.475 GHz\n         </span>\n         <sup>\n          3\n         </sup>\n        </td>\n        <td colspan="2">\n         <span class="nowrap">\n          3.300 GHz \xe2\x80\x93 3.500 GHz\n         </span>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td>\n         <b>\n          <a href="/wiki/5-centimeter_band" title="5-centimeter band">\n           5 cm\n          </a>\n         </b>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <span class="nowrap">\n          5.650 GHz \xe2\x80\x93 5.850 GHz\n         </span>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <span class="nowrap">\n          5.650 GHz \xe2\x80\x93 5.925 GHz\n         </span>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <span class="nowrap">\n          5.650 GHz \xe2\x80\x93 5.850 GHz\n         </span>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td>\n         <b>\n          <a href="/wiki/3-centimeter_band" title="3-centimeter band">\n           3 cm\n          </a>\n         </b>\n        </td>\n        <td colspan="3">\n         <span class="nowrap">\n          10.000 GHz \xe2\x80\x93 10.500 GHz\n         </span>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td>\n         <b>\n          <a href="/wiki/1.2-centimeter_band" title="1.2-centimeter band">\n           1.2 cm\n          </a>\n         </b>\n        </td>\n        <td colspan="3">\n         <span class="nowrap">\n          24.000 GHz \xe2\x80\x93 24.250 GHz\n         </span>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th rowspan="5">\n         <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Extremely_High_Frequency" title="Extremely High Frequency">\n          EHF\n         </a>\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         <b>\n          <a href="/wiki/6-millimeter_band" title="6-millimeter band">\n           6 mm\n          </a>\n         </b>\n        </td>\n        <td colspan="3">\n         <span class="nowrap">\n          47.000 GHz \xe2\x80\x93 47.200 GHz\n         </span>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td>\n         <b>\n          <a href="/wiki/4-millimeter_band" title="4-millimeter band">\n           4 mm\n          </a>\n         </b>\n         <sup>\n          3\n         </sup>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <span class="nowrap">\n          <i>\n           75.500 GHz\n          </i>\n          <sup>\n           1\n          </sup>\n          \xe2\x80\x93 81.500 GHz\n         </span>\n        </td>\n        <td colspan="2">\n         <span class="nowrap">\n          76.000 GHz \xe2\x80\x93 81.500 GHz\n         </span>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td>\n         <b>\n          <a href="/wiki/2.5-millimeter_band" title="2.5-millimeter band">\n           2.5 mm\n          </a>\n         </b>\n        </td>\n        <td colspan="3">\n         <span class="nowrap">\n          122.250 GHz \xe2\x80\x93 123.000 GHz\n         </span>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td>\n         <b>\n          <a href="/wiki/2-millimeter_band" title="2-millimeter band">\n           2 mm\n          </a>\n         </b>\n        </td>\n        <td colspan="3">\n         <span class="nowrap">\n          134.000 GHz \xe2\x80\x93 141.000 GHz\n         </span>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td>\n         <b>\n          <a href="/wiki/1-millimeter_band" title="1-millimeter band">\n           1 mm\n          </a>\n         </b>\n        </td>\n        <td colspan="3">\n         <span class="nowrap">\n          241.000 GHz \xe2\x80\x93 250.000 GHz\n         </span>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th>\n         <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Tremendously_high_frequency" title="Tremendously high frequency">\n          THF\n         </a>\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         <i>\n          <b>\n           <a href="/wiki/Submillimeter_amateur_radio" title="Submillimeter amateur radio">\n            Sub-mm\n           </a>\n          </b>\n         </i>\n        </td>\n        <td colspan="3">\n         <i>\n          Some administrations have authorized spectrum for amateur use in this region.\n         </i>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="5" style="text-align:left;background: lightskyblue">\n         <p>\n          <sup>\n           1\n          </sup>\n          This is not mentioned in the\n          <a href="/wiki/International_Telecommunication_Union" title="International Telecommunication Union">\n           ITU\n          </a>\n          \'s\n          <i>\n           Table of Frequency Allocations\n          </i>\n          , but individual administrations may make allocations under\n          <a class="external text" href="http://life.itu.int/radioclub/rr/frr.htm" rel="nofollow">\n           Article 4.4\n          </a>\n          of the ITU Radio Regulations. See the appropriate Wiki page for further information.\n          <br/>\n          <sup>\n           2\n          </sup>\n          HF allocation created at the 1979\n          <a href="/wiki/World_Administrative_Radio_Conference" title="World Administrative Radio Conference">\n           World Administrative Radio Conference\n          </a>\n          . These are commonly called the "\n          <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/WARC_band" title="WARC band">\n           WARC bands\n          </a>\n          ".\n          <br/>\n          <sup>\n           3\n          </sup>\n          This includes a currently active\n          <i>\n           footnote allocation\n          </i>\n          mentioned in the ITU\'s\n          <i>\n           Table of Frequency Allocations\n          </i>\n          . These allocations may only apply to a group of countries.\n         </p>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="5" style="text-align:center;background: skyblue">\n         See also:\n         <a href="/wiki/Template:Radio_spectrum" title="Template:Radio spectrum">\n          Radio spectrum\n         </a>\n         \xc2\xb7\n         <a href="/wiki/Template:Electromagnetic_spectrum" title="Template:Electromagnetic spectrum">\n          Electromagnetic spectrum\n         </a>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Modes_of_communication">\n        Modes of communication\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Amateur_radio&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: Modes of communication">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">\n       See also:\n       <a href="/wiki/List_of_amateur_radio_modes" title="List of amateur radio modes">\n        List of amateur radio modes\n       </a>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       Amateurs use a variety of voice, text, image, and data communications modes over radio. Generally new modes can be tested in the amateur radio service, although national regulations may require disclosure of a new mode to permit radio licensing authorities to monitor the transmissions.\n       <a href="/wiki/Encryption" title="Encryption">\n        Encryption\n       </a>\n       , for example, is not generally permitted in the Amateur Radio service except for the special purpose of satellite vehicle control uplinks. The following is a partial list of the modes of communication used, where the mode includes both\n       <a href="/wiki/Modulation" title="Modulation">\n        modulation\n       </a>\n       types and operating protocols.\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Voice">\n        Voice\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Amateur_radio&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: Voice">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <ul>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/Amplitude_modulation" title="Amplitude modulation">\n         Amplitude modulation\n        </a>\n        (AM)\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/Double-sideband_suppressed-carrier_transmission" title="Double-sideband suppressed-carrier transmission">\n         Double Sideband Suppressed Carrier\n        </a>\n        (DSB-SC)\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/Independent_sideband" title="Independent sideband">\n         Independent Sideband\n        </a>\n        (ISB)\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/Single-sideband_modulation" title="Single-sideband modulation">\n         Single Sideband\n        </a>\n        (SSB)\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Amplitude_modulation_equivalent" title="Amplitude modulation equivalent">\n         Amplitude Modulation Equivalent\n        </a>\n        (AME)\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/Frequency_modulation" title="Frequency modulation">\n         Frequency modulation\n        </a>\n        (FM)\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/Phase_modulation" title="Phase modulation">\n         Phase modulation\n        </a>\n        (PM)\n       </li>\n      </ul>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Image">\n        Image\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Amateur_radio&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: Image">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <ul>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/Amateur_television" title="Amateur television">\n         Amateur Television\n        </a>\n        (ATV), also known as\n        <i>\n         Fast Scan television\n        </i>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/Slow-scan_television" title="Slow-scan television">\n         Slow-Scan Television\n        </a>\n        (SSTV)\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/Radiofax" title="Radiofax">\n         Facsimile\n        </a>\n       </li>\n      </ul>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Text_and_data">\n        Text and data\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Amateur_radio&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: Text and data">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       Most amateur digital modes are transmitted by inserting audio into the microphone input of a radio and using an analog scheme, such as\n       <a href="/wiki/Amplitude_modulation" title="Amplitude modulation">\n        amplitude modulation\n       </a>\n       (AM),\n       <a href="/wiki/Frequency_modulation" title="Frequency modulation">\n        frequency modulation\n       </a>\n       (FM), or\n       <a href="/wiki/Single-sideband_modulation" title="Single-sideband modulation">\n        single-sideband modulation\n       </a>\n       (SSB).\n      </p>\n      <ul>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/Continuous_wave" title="Continuous wave">\n         Continuous Wave\n        </a>\n        (CW), usually used for\n        <a href="/wiki/Morse_code" title="Morse code">\n         Morse code\n        </a>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/Automatic_link_establishment" title="Automatic link establishment">\n         Automatic Link Establishment\n        </a>\n        (ALE)\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/AMTOR" title="AMTOR">\n         AMateur Teleprinting Over Radio\n        </a>\n        (AMTOR)\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/D-STAR" title="D-STAR">\n         D-STAR\n        </a>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/Digital_mobile_radio" title="Digital mobile radio">\n         Digital mobile radio\n        </a>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/EchoLink" title="EchoLink">\n         EchoLink\n        </a>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/Hellschreiber" title="Hellschreiber">\n         Hellschreiber\n        </a>\n        , also referred to as either\n        <i>\n         Feld-Hell\n        </i>\n        , or\n        <i>\n         Hell\n        </i>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Discrete_multi-tone_modulation" title="Discrete multi-tone modulation">\n         Discrete multi-tone modulation\n        </a>\n        modes such as\n        <a href="/wiki/MT63" title="MT63">\n         Multi Tone 63\n        </a>\n        (MT63)\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/Multiple_frequency-shift_keying" title="Multiple frequency-shift keying">\n         Multiple Frequency-Shift Keying\n        </a>\n        (MFSK) modes such as\n        <ul>\n         <li>\n          <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/WSJT_(Amateur_radio_software)" title="WSJT (Amateur radio software)">\n           FSK441, JT6M, JT65\n          </a>\n          , and\n         </li>\n         <li>\n          <a href="/wiki/WSPR_(amateur_radio_software)" title="WSPR (amateur radio software)">\n           WSPR\n          </a>\n         </li>\n         <li>\n          <a href="/wiki/Olivia_MFSK" title="Olivia MFSK">\n           Olivia MFSK\n          </a>\n         </li>\n        </ul>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/Packet_radio" title="Packet radio">\n         Packet radio\n        </a>\n        (\n        <a href="/wiki/AX.25" title="AX.25">\n         AX.25\n        </a>\n        )\n        <ul>\n         <li>\n          <a href="/wiki/Automatic_Packet_Reporting_System" title="Automatic Packet Reporting System">\n           Automatic Packet Reporting System\n          </a>\n          (APRS)\n         </li>\n        </ul>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/PACTOR" title="PACTOR">\n         PACTOR\n        </a>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/Phase-shift_keying" title="Phase-shift keying">\n         Phase-Shift Keying\n        </a>\n        <ul>\n         <li>\n          31\n          <a href="/wiki/Baud" title="Baud">\n           baud\n          </a>\n          <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/BPSK" title="BPSK">\n           binary phase shift keying\n          </a>\n          :\n          <a href="/wiki/PSK31" title="PSK31">\n           PSK31\n          </a>\n         </li>\n         <li>\n          31\n          <a href="/wiki/Baud" title="Baud">\n           baud\n          </a>\n          <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/QPSK" title="QPSK">\n           quadrature phase shift keying\n          </a>\n          :\n          <a href="/wiki/PSK31" title="PSK31">\n           QPSK31\n          </a>\n         </li>\n         <li>\n          63\n          <a href="/wiki/Baud" title="Baud">\n           baud\n          </a>\n          <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/BPSK" title="BPSK">\n           binary phase shift keying\n          </a>\n          :\n          <a href="/wiki/PSK63" title="PSK63">\n           PSK63\n          </a>\n         </li>\n         <li>\n          63\n          <a href="/wiki/Baud" title="Baud">\n           baud\n          </a>\n          <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/QPSK" title="QPSK">\n           quadrature phase shift keying\n          </a>\n          :\n          <a href="/wiki/PSK63" title="PSK63">\n           QPSK63\n          </a>\n         </li>\n        </ul>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/Spread_spectrum" title="Spread spectrum">\n         Spread spectrum\n        </a>\n        (SS)\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/Radioteletype" title="Radioteletype">\n         Radioteletype\n        </a>\n        (RTTY)\n       </li>\n      </ul>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Modes_by_activity">\n        Modes by activity\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Amateur_radio&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Modes by activity">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       The following "modes" use no one specific modulation scheme but rather are classified by the activity of the communication.\n      </p>\n      <ul>\n       <li>\n        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/EME_(communications)" title="EME (communications)">\n         Earth-Moon-Earth\n        </a>\n        (EME)\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/Internet_Radio_Linking_Project" title="Internet Radio Linking Project">\n         Internet Radio Linking Project\n        </a>\n        (IRLP)\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/QRP_operation" title="QRP operation">\n         Low Transmitter Power\n        </a>\n        (QRP)\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/Amateur_radio_satellite" title="Amateur radio satellite">\n         Satellite\n        </a>\n        (OSCAR \xe2\x80\x93 Orbiting Satellite Carrying Amateur Radio)\n       </li>\n      </ul>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="See_also">\n        See also\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n
